FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [a].[Id], [a].[AccessFailedCount], [a].[ApplicationId], [a].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a].[Email], [a].[EmailConfirmed], [a].[FirstName], [a].[LastName], [a].[LockoutEnabled], [a].[LockoutEnd], [a].[NormalizedEmail], [a].[NormalizedUserName], [a].[PasswordHash], [a].[PhoneNumber], [a].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a].[RefreshToken], [a].[RefreshTokenExpiryTime], [a].[SecurityStamp], [a].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a].[UserName]
    FROM [AspNetUsers] AS [a]
    WHERE [a].[UserName] = @__userName_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a0].[UserId], [a0].[RoleId], [a0].[AssignedDate], [a1].[Id], [a1].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a1].[Description], [a1].[Name], [a1].[NormalizedName]
    FROM [AspNetUserRoles] AS [a0]

) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[UserId]

FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [a].[Id], [a].[AccessFailedCount], [a].[ApplicationId], [a].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a].[Email], [a].[EmailConfirmed], [a].[FirstName], [a].[LastName], [a].[LockoutEnabled], [a].[LockoutEnd], [a].[NormalizedEmail], [a].[NormalizedUserName], [a].[PasswordHash], [a].[PhoneNumber], [a].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a].[RefreshToken], [a].[RefreshTokenExpiryTime], [a].[SecurityStamp], [a].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a].[UserName]
    FROM [AspNetUsers] AS [a]
    WHERE [a].[UserName] = @__userName_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a0].[UserId], [a0].[RoleId], [a0].[AssignedDate], [a1].[Id], [a1].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a1].[Description], [a1].[Name], [a1].[NormalizedName]
    FROM [AspNetUserRoles] AS [a0]
    INNER JOIN [AspNetRoles] AS [a1] ON [a0].[RoleId] = [a1].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[UserId]

    SELECT TOP(1) [a].[Id], [a].[AccessFailedCount], [a].[ApplicationId], [a].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a].[Email], [a].[EmailConfirmed], [a].[FirstName], [a].[LastName], [a].[LockoutEnabled], [a].[LockoutEnd], [a].[NormalizedEmail], [a].[NormalizedUserName], [a].[PasswordHash], [a].[PhoneNumber], [a].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a].[RefreshToken], [a].[RefreshTokenExpiryTime], [a].[SecurityStamp], [a].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a].[UserName]

FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [a].[Id], [a].[AccessFailedCount], [a].[ApplicationId], [a].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a].[Email], [a].[EmailConfirmed], [a].[FirstName], [a].[LastName], [a].[LockoutEnabled], [a].[LockoutEnd], [a].[NormalizedEmail], [a].[NormalizedUserName], [a].[PasswordHash], [a].[PhoneNumber], [a].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a].[RefreshToken], [a].[RefreshTokenExpiryTime], [a].[SecurityStamp], [a].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a].[UserName]

) AS [t]

FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [a].[Id], [a].[AccessFailedCount], [a].[ApplicationId], [a].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a].[Email], [a].[EmailConfirmed], [a].[FirstName], [a].[LastName], [a].[LockoutEnabled], [a].[LockoutEnd], [a].[NormalizedEmail], [a].[NormalizedUserName], [a].[PasswordHash], [a].[PhoneNumber], [a].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a].[RefreshToken], [a].[RefreshTokenExpiryTime], [a].[SecurityStamp], [a].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a].[UserName]
    FROM [AspNetUsers] AS [a]
    WHERE [a].[UserName] = @__userName_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a0].[UserId], [a0].[RoleId], [a0].[AssignedDate], [a1].[Id], [a1].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a1].[Description], [a1].[Name], [a1].[NormalizedName]
